Say Cheese has great products, but it seems that the staff are having issues. I went in to get a sandwich on Sunday, 7/19 at just around 2pm. As as I walked in, a worker passed by me on the way to take his break I'd later learn. One of the staff, older than the other guys and with long hair, was upset that that worker went on break allegedly without saying anything. He yelled at the other two workers loudly complaining that he was saddled with all of the responsibilities and that no one helped him clean. He also reprimanded them harshly for changing the radio station, "Nobody has time to help me, but everyone has time to play DJ!"

It's understandable to get upset when you perceive that your coworkers are not pulling their weight, but to yell and swear loudly (F bombs and the like) while there are customers present is frankly unacceptable. I'll continue to shop here, and I give the food 4 stars, but that last visit made me really uncomfortable.</text>

< Review>
My daughter and I thought the birria was delicious! Very authentic.

I must have literally driven past this restaurant without noticing it hundreds of times over the years. It is very easy to miss; small, no flashy sign, and just blends into the little strip of business where it is located. It is not a fancy, but we were treated very well by the family who owns and operates this business. The service and food were both great, and I will definitely be going back again!<//Review>

<user_id>111574532729357790876< /user_id>< name>
Andrew Chang<//name>
<Date>1542667094540</Date>< rating>
4</rating>
< text>
Mexican spot tucked at the end of a small strip mall sharing the parking lot with a sports bar and liquor store. I was the only one who wasn't speaking Spanish while I was there.

As their name implies, birria is their specialty with Birria de Res (beef) and Birria de Chivo (goat) available in both seca (dry) and caldo (soup) forms. Menudo and pozole also are listed under Specialties  and other Mexican standards are on the menu like burritos, tacos, enchiladas, and tortas.

The Caldo version comes with corn tortillas, lemon and lime wedges, and topped with onions, cilantro and salsa. The broth is flavorful and mildly spicy. The goat meat was tender and not too gamey.

I liked it, but thought it was a little pricey at just under $13.

Friendly service.<//text>

<Rating>5<//Rating><Text>Just had lunch here. The owner was very nice and the service was fast. I got the vegetarian plate, which is a great deal - comes out at about $10 after tax and includes a drink. I'm a big fan of Lebanese food - I basically go around trying out different places' vegetarian plates - and while I can't say this place is the absolute best I've ever had in my whole life, it's very good. And that's especially so considering the price.

Tabbouleh was nice and lemony, hummus was creamy, falafel were crispy on the outside and soft inside - basically, everything in order! I particularly liked the tahini dipping sauce - more flavorful than what you get at other places, there's definitely something extra in there although I'm not sure what. The dolmeh was good - but I guess I'm a little spoiled because I'm used to vegetarian plates coming with more than one :)

I also got a spinach pie to go - again, a little spoiled as I'm used to that coming with the vegetarian plate. But now I see why - this place's pies are huge, basically a full meal (comes with tzatziki). It was cooked fresh for me just like the falafel. Nice and lemony filling. They made the pie with the same flatbread that was served with the plate, which I guess gives you a break from phyllo dough if that's what you're used to - and also lets you eat it as a handheld meal if that's what you're after.<//Text><pics>None< /pics><response>None<//response>< gmap_id>

< review>
This was THE best office visit in the entire time I have been coming - MANY months, now! I was thrilled with the work done for me by Ceicali. She took such great care to keep me pain free. Opening the brackets is sometimes a chore - they do not want to let go. She performed that task in a way that did not give me more pain. She had to remove two brackets and reposition them as well as add another bracket where none had been. This often hurts, but not this time! She also put "chain" on both the top and bottom and for once I could actually get the floss-threader under the chain to clean my teeth. I didn't know it was possible to have a space to easily get the floss between teeth. She apologized to me because she said I would be hurting later, but the pain was minimal. I am so appreciative of you all.</review>

Dr. Lauritzen's office is THE BEST OFFICE IN TOWN and possibly all around!!!! Friendly staff, clean environment, and overall a lovely place to be! My experience with braces was great! She asks me about my son, my life, and knows how to keep a conversation going. Bring her Ferrero Rocher, it's her favorite :) Melissa and I were pregnant at the same time which was neat. We had a lot to talk about. Her son and my son have the same name. I thought that was cool! Debbie Debbie, very sweet lady. I love her personality! Ceicali usually gets to hear me make excuses and complain about my teeth, LOL! Nonnie & I talk about life in general. Mary is wonderful and helped me with all the finances. Tina is the sweetest receptionist. I usually don't leave right away; we talk and catch up before I head out the door. Many places makes you want to run out the door and never return. Marisela has such a bubbly personality and she has such beautiful hair, haha. I have not worked with Mandy, however, I am sure she is as wonderful as everyone else. These ladies have become family. You DO NOT find many offices that communicates well with you. Last but not least, Dr. Lauritzen. HE IS THE COOLEST and he really knows his stuff! You can totally tell he loves his job! Super friendly, hilarious, and all around a great individual! Customer Service is where it's at and this team's got it!<//review>

< text>
Awesome, healthy, vegetarian food. I was so sad when they stopped serving their teriyaki salmon! It used to come with grilled veggies, a salad, brown rice, and sooooooooo much of that good teriyaki sauce! PLEASE add this to your menu again, my family loves it and I want other people to get to enjoy it too!
The rest of the food here is equally good (once my family finished mourning their favorite dish, they instantly found a new group of favorites...aka the whole menu). The vegetarian/vegan options are totally great! I haven't eaten meat in so long that I don't remember what a burger tastes like, but even over all that time I just haven't been able to make a meal of some of the overly-healthy vegan food that some places serve. I mean, I just don't feel full unless I have a protein, you know? So I was super happy when my family found this place, because they had super good falafels (which are really filling), a lot of their non-mean dishes incorporate beans and other protein-packed legumes, and overall their vegetarian dishes are super comforting while still being healthy and ethical! The omnivores in my family always talk loudly about how good the meat dishes are, so this place is perfect for everyone!
Oh, not to mention they serve KILLER breakfasts!< /text>

< text>
Met an old friend here that I haven't seen in approx. ten years. My salad was good quality and our waitress was nice, not overbearing like some can be. She was kind enough to realize that we were catching up on old times and didn't come to our table too often (an art that some people in service don't pick up.) She was still attentive and we enjoyed our meal. We sat outside and besides the restaurant being on a busy road, it was surprisingly peaceful. Would like to return again to have breakfast (my favorite meal of the day) and really dig in :) Will return.<//text>

< Review>
Food, meh. Service, not good.

Ordered the spinach quesadilla, which the menu says to allow an extra 10 minutes for.  Apparantly this message didnt get to the wait staff because our entree arrived about 3 minutes after the app.  (At least this explains the unwillingness of our waitress to change my wife's order 3 minutes after we put it in - we thought that with an extra 10 minutes it wouldnt be an issue... it was).

I ordered the chicken shwarma which was a gluey purple mess with about 5 pieces of chicken in it.  Not nearly enough of the thin, dry, burnt pita to eat it with.  Overall a poor presentation for a weak dish.

My wife had the veggie kebab (she tried to change out for a veggie burger which we didnt see on the front of the menu initially,  but this could not be accommodated. Even just a few minutes after ordering and well before our app).  It was ok.  It says there is pineapple in it, and the tiny piece we found between everything else makes it true (but hardly worth a mention in the menu).  1 kebab, a ton of flavorless,  mushy brown rice, and mediocre hummus and mushy  sides.  Overall, not great.

< Text>
This place is hard to describe.  It's kind of a health food restaurant. You can get hummus and falafel.   It's open for dinner but I like it better for breakfast or lunch.  They do serve wine.  They also have a large tea menu.   There's outside seating that is fantastic 3/4 of the year and faces a large park.  This is a great place to go before or after spending time in Howarth Park/Spring Lake/Annadel. Also a great place to have dinner and a glass before you WALK to the movie theater next door.</Text>
